19 import akka.actor.ActorRef
20 import akka.http.scaladsl.server.Route

29 /**
30   * Service to handle the account of the user
31   */
32 trait UserRestService
33     extends UserRestServiceHandler
34     with HttpUtility
35     with LazyLogging
36     with Constants {
37   // ==============================
38   //     REST ROUTES
39   // ==============================
40 
41   /**
42     * user routes
43     * @param actor
44     * @return Route
45     */
46 
47   def userRoutes(actor: ActorRef): Route =
48     pathPrefix("user") {
49       get {
50         path("get-all-users") {
51           val result =
52             getUserDetails(actor)
53           logDuration(complete(result))
54         } }~
55       delete{    path("delete-customer") {
56             parameters('userId.?) { (userId: Option[String]) =>
57               val result =
58                 deleteUser(actor, userId)
59               logDuration(complete(result))
60             }
61           }
62       } ~
63         pathPrefix("insert-user") {
64           pathEnd {
65             (put & entity(as[UserDetails])) { userDetails =>
66               logger.info("add user details " + userDetails)
67               val result =
68                 addUserDetails(actor, userDetails)
69               logDuration(complete(result))
70             }
71           }
72         } ~
73         pathPrefix("update-admin-username") {
74           pathEnd {
75             (put & entity(as[UpdateAdminUsername])) { adminDetails =>
76               logger.info("update admin username " + adminDetails)
77               val result =
78                 updateAdminUsername(actor, adminDetails)
79               logDuration(complete(result))
80             }
81           }
82         }
83     }
84 
85   def routes(command: ActorRef): Route =
86     userRoutes(command)
87 }
